        <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-salesforce-lead-to-order" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#salesforce-lead-to-order"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Salesforce Lead-To-Order</h1>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-table-of-contents" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#table-of-contents"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Table of contents</h2>

<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-general-solution-description" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#general-solution-description"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>General solution description</h2>
<p dir="auto">This connector generates a process mining model for Salesforce Lead-To-Order (L2O).</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-source-system" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#source-system"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Source system</h3>
<p dir="auto">Salesforce Sales Cloud.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-process" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#process"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Process</h3>
<p dir="auto">The Lead To Order process is a end to end process which starts with a potential customer's intent to buy a product, up to the fullfilment of this sale.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/UiPath/ProcessMining-TemplateOne-L2O-Salesforce-connector/blob/main/documentation/img/Lead-To-Order-High-Level-Process.png"><img src="/UiPath/ProcessMining-TemplateOne-L2O-Salesforce-connector/raw/main/documentation/img/Lead-To-Order-High-Level-Process.png" alt="alt text" title="Lead To Order High Level Process" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Lead Qualification</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Once a lead is generated, the lead will go through a qualification process. The objective of this process is to determine whether the lead is most likely to make an actual purchase. Once the lead is qualified this will turn into an actual opportunity for a sale. In Salesforce, this is tracked via the <code>Lead</code> object.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Opportunity Management</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">As a lead qualifies into an opportunity, the sales team will work on the opportunity together with the potential customer, in order to identify the need and suggest an appropiate product or service which will meet this need. Part of the process may involve generating a quote to the customer, but this is not always the case. In case the opportunity is won, this will generate one or more orders in order to fulfill the won opportunity. In Salesforce, this is tracked via the <code>Opportunity</code> object, and optionally, the <code>Quote</code> object.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Order Management</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Within Order management, the order lifecycle is maintained, including order capture, and fulfillment. In Salesforce, the <code>Order</code> object is used to maintain this process. One opportunity may have multiple orders.</p>
<p dir="auto">Optionally, this may then extend and generate an invoice and receivables, in what is called the <strong>Lead to Cash</strong> process.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-connector-output--compatability" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#connector-output--compatability"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Connector output &amp; compatability</h3>
<p dir="auto">The connector is built for use with TemplateOne, and has the possibility to expand case and event attributes as required.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-prerequisites" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#prerequisites"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Prerequisites</h2>
<p dir="auto">Depending on which fields have field history tracked, different change events will be recorded. Field history tracking can be configured from each object within Salesforce setup.
Recommended minimal setup is having the following object and fields tracked:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Opportunity: Stagename</li>
<li>Lead: Status</li>
<li>Order: Status</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Additional events are included as part of field tracking history, however the connector is built so additional events are customized based on requirements.</p>
<p dir="auto">By default, Field History is disabled per object. In order to setup Field History Tracking for an object, the following Salesforce manual contains a step by step instruction: <a href="https://developer.salesforce.com/docs/atlas.en-us.securityImplGuide.meta/securityImplGuide/tracking_field_history_for_standard_objects.htm" rel="nofollow">Salesforce - Track Field History for Standard Objects</a>. Please note that if a field is activated for tracking, the values will be tracked from that moment onwards. Any changes before that point in time will not be saved. As of February 2022, Salesforce retains field history data for up to 18 months through the org and up to 24 months via the API, and Field history tracking data doesn’t count towards Salesforce org’s data storage limits.</p>
<p dir="auto">In case the history needs to be stored for a longer period of time, <a href="https://developer.salesforce.com/docs/atlas.en-us.securityImplGuide.meta/securityImplGuide/field_audit_trail.htm" rel="nofollow">Field Audit Trail</a> must be activated. This allows copying of history data into a separate big data object and allows storage for up to 10 years.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-environmental-settings" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#environmental-settings"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Environmental settings</h3>
<p dir="auto">In order to connect via CData, the user establishing the connection must be API Enabled, and must have appropiate read permissions on each of the objects which are being extracted. All fields included in the input tables must be visible for the user extracting the data. In case any fields are not visible, and may not be made visible, permissions should be granted to the user, or a profile with permissions should be used to extract the data.</p>
<p dir="auto">Additionally, the user must be marked as "Marketing User" in the user settings in order to extract Campaign information.</p>
<p dir="auto">In order to calculate amounts using historical exchange rates, Effective dated currency should be enabled in the Salesforce org, and historical exchange rates should be loaded into the system.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-system-specific-settings" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#system-specific-settings"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>System specific settings</h3>
<p dir="auto">The Salesforce Lead to Order connector works on the process starting on the marketing campaign generation, up to the generation of customer orders.</p>
<p dir="auto">This includes processing of the following Salesforce transactional objects:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Campaign</li>
<li>CampaignMember</li>
<li>Lead</li>
<li>LeadHistory</li>
<li>Opportunity</li>
<li>OpportunityFieldHistory</li>
<li>Quote*</li>
<li>Order*</li>
<li>OrderHistory*</li>
<li>ProcessInstance</li>
<li>ProcessInstanceStep</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">The following additional objects which are used to add additional attribute information into the model:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Account</li>
<li>RecordType</li>
<li>User</li>
<li>ProcessDefinition</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">In case they are used, the following tables add Currency conversion to the model:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>CurrencyType*</li>
<li>DatedExchangeRate*</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">*<code>Quote</code>, <code>Order</code>, <code>OrderHistory</code>, <code>CurrencyType</code>, <code>DatedExchangeRate</code> objects are by default disabled in Salesforce orgs. By default, these will not be considered in the transformations. If these are used, the transformation and related logic can be enabled by using DBT variables. The details to configure these options are described in the <a href="#Connector-configuration">Connector configuration</a> section, and in the <a href="#Extraction">Extraction</a> section.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-extraction" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#extraction"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Extraction</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-load-from-source-data-extraction--connection-to-source-system" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#load-from-source-data-extraction--connection-to-source-system"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Load from Source Data extraction &amp; connection to source system</h3>
<p dir="auto">Detailed instructions for extractions can be found in the following document: <a href="/UiPath/ProcessMining-TemplateOne-L2O-Salesforce-connector/blob/main/extractors/load-from-source/instructions.md">Load from Source Extraction</a></p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-load-from-file-data-import" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#load-from-file-data-import"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Load from File Data Import</h3>
<p dir="auto">Detailed instructions for extractions can be found in the following document: <a href="/UiPath/ProcessMining-TemplateOne-L2O-Salesforce-connector/blob/main/extractors/load-from-file/instructions.md">Load from File Extraction</a></p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-input-data" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#input-data"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Input data</h3>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Account</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Represents an individual account, which is an organization or person involved with your business (such as customers, competitors, and partners).</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Field</th>
<th align="left">Stores</th>
<th align="left">Filtering</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">Id</td>
<td align="left">Account Identifier (Primary Key)</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">AccountSource</td>
<td align="left">The source of the account record. For example, Advertisement, Data.com, or Trade Show. The source is selected from a picklist of available values, which are set by an administrator.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">BillingCountry</td>
<td align="left">Details for the billing address of this account.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">BillingState</td>
<td align="left">Details for the billing address of this account.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">CreatedById</td>
<td align="left">User ID who created the account.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">CreatedDate</td>
<td align="left">Date in which the account was created.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Industry</td>
<td align="left">An industry associated with this account.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">IsPersonAccount*</td>
<td align="left">Indicates whether this account has a record type of Person Account (true) or not (false). <em>This field is not available by default in Salesforce, but is setup by Salesforce when requested for B2C environments. This attribute can be enabled / disabled using the <code>use_is_person_account</code> DBT variable</em> .</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Name</td>
<td align="left">Name of the account. If the account has a record type of Person Account: This value is the concatenation of the FirstName, MiddleName, LastName, and Suffix of the associated person contact.</td>
<td align="left"></td>

<tr>

<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Rating</td>
<td align="left">The account’s prospect rating, for example Hot, Warm, or Cold.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Type</td>
<td align="left">Type of account, for example, Customer, Competitor, or Partner.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<p dir="auto"><strong>CurrencyType</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Represents the currencies used by an organization for which the multicurrency feature is enabled.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Field</th>
<th align="left">Stores</th>
<th align="left">Filtering</th>
</tr>
</thead>

<td align="left">Currency Type record identifier (Primary Key).</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">IsoCode</td>
<td align="left">ISO code of the currency. Must be one of the valid alphabetic, three-letter currency ISO codes defined by the ISO 4217 standard, such as USD, GBP, or JPY.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">IsCorporate</td>
<td align="left">Indicates whether this currency type is the corporate currency (true) or not (false). Label is Corporate Currency. All other currency conversion rates are applied against this corporate currency.</td>
<td align="left">= 1</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>DatedConversionRate</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Represents the dated exchange rates used by an organization for which the multicurrency and the effective dated currency features are enabled.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Field</th>
<th align="left">Stores</th>
</tr>

<td align="left">Dated Conversion Rate record identifier (Primary Key).</td>

<td align="left">ISO code of the currency. Must be one of the valid alphabetic, three-letter currency ISO codes defined by the ISO 4217 standard, such as USD, GBP, or JPY.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">StartDate</td>
<td align="left">The date on which the effective dated exchange rate starts.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">NextStarteDate</td>
<td align="left">The date on which the next effective dated exchange rate will start. Effectively the day after the end date for this exchange rate.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">ConversionRate</td>
<td align="left">Conversion rate of this currency type against the corporate currency.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Opportunity</strong> <em>(Main Object)</em></p>

<tr>
<th align="left">Field</th>
<th align="left">Stores</th>
<th align="left">Filtering</th>

<td align="left"></td>
</tr>

<td align="left"></td>
</tr>

<td align="left">ID of the User who has been assigned to work this opportunity.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>

<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">RecordTypeId*</td>
<td align="left">ID of the record type assigned to this object. <em>In order for this field to appear on the opportunity object, there needs to be at least one record type for opportunities.</em></td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">StageName</td>
<td align="left">Current stage of this record. The StageName field controls several other fields on an opportunity.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Type</td>
<td align="left">Type of opportunity. For example, Existing Business or New Business.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Order</strong></p>

<td align="left"></td>

<td align="left">Main field used for time-based filtering</td>

<td align="left"></td>
</tr>

<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>OrderHistory</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Represents historical information about changes that have been made to the standard fields of the associated order, or to any custom fields with history tracking enabled.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Field</th>
<th align="left">Stores</th>
<th align="left">Filtering</th>
</tr>
</thead>

<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">IsDeleted</td>
<td align="left">Flags whether the Order history record was deleted.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">OrderId</td>
<td align="left">Related order Record Id.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">CreatedById</td>
<td align="left">User ID who created the history record.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">CreatedDate</td>
<td align="left">Date in which the history record was created.</td>
<td align="left">Main field used for time-based filtering</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">DataType</td>
<td align="left">Data Type for the field which was modified.</td>
<td align="left">&lt;&gt; 'EntityId'</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Field</td>
<td align="left">Field which was modified on the order record.</td>
<td align="left">in ('Status','Owner','TotalAmount')</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">OldValue</td>
<td align="left">Value before change.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">NewValue</td>
<td align="left">Value after change.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Quote</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The Quote object represents a quote, which is a record showing proposed prices for products and services.
Quotes can be created from and synced with opportunities, and emailed as PDFs to customers.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Field</th>
<th align="left">Stores</th>
<th align="left">Filtering</th>
</tr>

<td align="left"></td>
</tr>

<td align="left">CreatedById</td>
<td align="left">User ID who created the quote.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">CreatedDate</td>
<td align="left">Date in which the quote was created.</td>
<td align="left">Main field used for time-based filtering</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Name</td>
<td align="left">Name for the quote.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">OpportunityId</td>
<td align="left">ID for the opportunity associated with the quote.</td>
<td align="left"></td>
</tr>

<p dir="auto"><strong>ProcessDefinition</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Represents the definition of a single approval process.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Stores</th>
<th>Filtering</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Id</td>
<td>Record Type Identifier (Primary Key).</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Name</td>
<td>The unique process name, used internally.</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>TableEnumOrId</td>
<td>Specifies the object associated with the approval process, such as Account or Contact.</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Type</td>
<td>The type of this process. Approval Process—Used to control the action taken for a record. State-based Process—Used internally to track various control processes, such as for developing Salesforce Knowledge articles.</td>
<td>= 'Approval'</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>ProcessInstance</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Represents an instance of a single, end-to-end approval process.</p>

<th>Field</th>
<th>Stores</th>
<th>Filtering</th>
</tr>

<tr>

<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CreatedDate</td>
<td>Date in which the process instance was created.</td>
<td>Main field used for time-based filtering</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Status</td>
<td>The status of this approval process instance, for example Started, Pending, or Approved.</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ProcessDefinitionId</td>
<td>The ID of this approval process instance. This is a relationship field</td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>TargetObjectId</td>

<td></td>
</tr>

</table>

<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-connector-design" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#connector-design"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Connector design</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-entities" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#entities"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Entities</h3>
<p dir="auto">Salesforce already treats each object as an individual entity, however the objects are joined to additional master data in order to provide additional information.</p>

<td align="left">Opportunity, Accounts, User, RecordType</td>
</tr>
<tr>

<td align="left">Quote, User</td>

<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-activities" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#activities"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Activities</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Entity</th>
<th align="left">Activity</th>
<th align="left">Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">Lead</td>
<td align="left">Creation</td>
<td align="left">Lead is generated in the system. Identified based on the <code>CreateDate</code> field on the <code>Lead</code> object.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Lead</td>
<td align="left">Add to Campaign</td>
<td align="left">Lead is added to a marketing campaign for tracking. Identified based on the <code>CreateDate</code> field on the <code>CampaignMember</code> object for each LeadId.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Lead</td>
<td align="left">Status Change*</td>
<td align="left">Lead moves from different status. Standard status in Salesforce are: Open, Contacted, Qualified, Unqualified. Identified based on the Old and New values for <code>field</code> = <code>Status</code> on the <code>LeadHistory</code> object.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Lead</td>
<td align="left">Approvals*</td>
<td align="left">Any approval process which was submitted. This may be generated by any custom configuration the customer has.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Lead</td>
<td align="left">Additional Field Changes*</td>
<td align="left">Depending on fields tracked on the object, the event will be record as a change activity. In the standard connector, <code>Owner</code> and <code>Rating</code> are tracked, but may be expanded depending on customer configuration. Identified based on records on the <code>LeadHistory</code> object.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Opportunity</td>
<td align="left">Creation</td>
<td align="left">Opportunity is generated in the system. Identified based on the <code>CreateDate</code> field on the <code>Opportunity</code> object.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Opportunity</td>
<td align="left">Stage Change*</td>
<td align="left">Opportunity moves from different status. Standard status in Salesforce are: Prospecting, Qualification, Needs Analysis, Value Proposition, ID Decision Makers, Perception Analysis, Proposal / Price Quote, Negotiation / Review, Closed Won, Closed Lost. Identified based on the Old and New values for <code>field</code> = <code>StageName</code> on the <code>OpportunityFieldHistory</code> object.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Opportunity</td>
<td align="left">Additional Changes*</td>
<td align="left">Depending on fields tracked on the object, the event will be record as a change activity. In the standard connector, <code>Owner</code>, <code>Close Date</code> and <code>Amount</code> are tracked, but may be expanded depending on customer configuration. Identified based on values on the <code>OpportunityFieldHistory</code> object.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Opportunity</td>
<td align="left">Approvals*</td>
<td align="left">Any approval process which was submitted. This may be generated by any custom configuration the customer has.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Quote</td>
<td align="left">Creation</td>
<td align="left">Quote is generated in the system. Identified based on the <code>CreateDate</code> field on the <code>Quote</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Quote</td>
<td align="left">Approvals*</td>
<td align="left">Any approval process which was submitted. This may be generated by any custom configuration the customer has.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Order</td>
<td align="left">Creation</td>
<td align="left">Order is generated in the system. Identified based on the <code>CreateDate</code> field on the <code>Order</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Order</td>
<td align="left">Status Change*</td>
<td align="left">Order moves from different status. Standard status in Salesforce are: Draft, Activated. Identified based on the Old and New values for <code>field = Status</code> on the <code>OrderHistory</code> object.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Order</td>
<td align="left">Additional Changes*</td>
<td align="left">Depending on fields tracked on the object, the event will be record as a change activity. In the standard connector, Owner, and TotalAmount are tracked, but may be expanded depending on customer configuration. Identified based on the values on the <code>OrderHistory</code> object.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Order</td>
<td align="left">Approvals*</td>
<td align="left">Any approval process which was submitted. This may be generated by any custom configuration the customer has.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto">*The actual activity names will depend on the values defined on the customer Salesforce organization.</p>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Events</strong></p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Field</th>
<th align="left">Data Type</th>
<th align="left">Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">Case_ID</td>
<td align="left">Text</td>
<td align="left">The unique identifier of the case. Mandatory field.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Activity</td>
<td align="left">Text</td>
<td align="left">The name of the event. This describes the step in the process. Mandatory Field.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Event_end</td>
<td align="left">Date Time</td>
<td align="left">The timestamp associated with the end of executing the event. Mandatory Field.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Activity_Type*</td>
<td align="left">Text</td>
<td align="left">Type of activity.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Activity_Order</td>
<td align="left">Integer</td>
<td align="left">If activities take place on the same time (in parallel), you can define their order here.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Automated</td>
<td align="left">Boolean</td>
<td align="left">Indicates whether the event is manually executed or automated.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Event_cost</td>
<td align="left">Double</td>
<td align="left">The costs for executing the event.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Event_Detail</td>
<td align="left">Text</td>
<td align="left">Information related to the event.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Event_ID</td>
<td align="left">Integer</td>
<td align="left">A unique identifier of the event.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Event_processing_time</td>
<td align="left">Integer</td>
<td align="left">The amount of time actually spent working for the event given in milliseconds.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Team</td>
<td align="left">Text</td>
<td align="left">The team that executed the event.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">User</td>
<td align="left">Text</td>
<td align="left">The user who executed the event.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">User_type*</td>
<td align="left">Text</td>
<td align="left">User Type – Related to the Salesforce License.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto">*Event attributes which need to be configured on top of standard TemplateOne event attributes.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-business-data-configuration" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#business-data-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Business data configuration</h3>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Tags</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Current out of the box tags initially require no configuration, but in case any custom activity names are used, they should be added into the Tags_preprocessing transformation in addition or replacing current values.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Tag</th>
<th align="left">Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">Opportunity amount reduced</td>
<td align="left">Opportunity Amount was changed to a value less than the original value. Represents an opportunity which is losing value.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Opportunity won without a Quote</td>
<td align="left">An opportunity was won without sending a formal quote. Potentially arriving to a tentative price or list of products could have improved chances.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Multiple Owner Changes</td>
<td align="left">Applies for all entities, reflects a back and forth between team members which may be justified (vacations, escalations) or may require attention.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Approval process started multiple times</td>
<td align="left">Multiple approvals may exist for one entity, however if the same approval process is triggered multiple times, there might be inefficiencies to review.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Opportunity close date postponed</td>
<td align="left">An opportunity is getting delayed according to it's original close date, which means the opportunity might require attention.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Due Dates</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Current out of the box due dates initially require no configuration, but in case any custom due dates names are used, they should be added or changed into the Due_dates_preprocessing transformation in addition or replacing current values.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Due date</th>
<th align="left">Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">Original Opportunity Close Date</td>
<td align="left">Identifies original expected close date for the opportunity and verifies against the actual close date.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-connector-design-diagrams" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#connector-design-diagrams"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Connector design diagrams</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-connector-design-flowchart" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#connector-design-flowchart"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Connector design flowchart</h3>
<p dir="auto">The data flow diagram shown below was generated automatically using <code>dbt docs generate</code> and <code>dbt docs serve</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/UiPath/ProcessMining-TemplateOne-L2O-Salesforce-connector/blob/main/documentation/img/data-flow.png"><img src="/UiPath/ProcessMining-TemplateOne-L2O-Salesforce-connector/raw/main/documentation/img/data-flow.png" alt="alt text" title="Connector Design Flowchart" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-entity-relationship-diagram" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#entity-relationship-diagram"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Entity relationship diagram</h3>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/UiPath/ProcessMining-TemplateOne-L2O-Salesforce-connector/blob/main/documentation/img/Entity-Relations.png"><img src="/UiPath/ProcessMining-TemplateOne-L2O-Salesforce-connector/raw/main/documentation/img/Entity-Relations.png" alt="alt text" title="Entity relationship diagram" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-connector-design-details" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#connector-design-details"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Connector design details</h2>
<p dir="auto">In order to add data which will be defined by the end user, two additional files are loaded into the model which need to be prepared by the customer. These files must be replaced by customer specific setup.</p>
<p dir="auto">This includes the <code>Event Processing Estimates</code> file, which contains <code>event cost</code> and <code>estimated processing time</code> for each activity, and the <code>Automated Users</code> file, which contains a list of users which are considered automated.</p>
<p dir="auto">In order to run the end to end process correctly, <code>dbt seed</code> should be run before <code>dbt run</code>, or alternatively, <code>dbt build</code> should be used always in order to consider data and test dependencies altogether.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-how-to-extend-the-connector" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-to-extend-the-connector"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>How to extend the connector</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-connector-configuration" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#connector-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Connector configuration</h3>
<p dir="auto"><strong>CData Variables</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Instructions on how to setup variables in CData can be found in the <a href="/UiPath/ProcessMining-TemplateOne-L2O-Salesforce-connector/blob/main/extractors/load-from-source/instructions.md">Load from Source Extraction</a> and <a href="/UiPath/ProcessMining-TemplateOne-L2O-Salesforce-connector/blob/main/extractors/load-from-file/instructions.md">Load from File Extraction</a> sections</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Connector DBT Variables</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The connector includes a series of variables that must be configured based on the Salesforce configuration for the end customer. These variables are defined in the <code>dbt_project.yml</code> file.</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Variable</th>
<th align="left">Type</th>
<th align="left">Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">schema_sources</td>
<td align="left">string</td>
<td align="left">Specifies the schema in the database where the source tables will be located.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">date_format</td>
<td align="left">string / Integer</td>
<td align="left">Specifies the date format which will be used when converting to <code>Date</code> type. SQL Server format value is <code>23</code>. Snowflake format value is <code>'YYYY-MM-DD'</code>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">time_format</td>
<td align="left">string / Integer</td>
<td align="left">Specifies the date format which will be used when converting to <code>Time</code> type. SQL Server format value is <code>8</code>. Snowflake format value is <code>'hh24:mi:ss'</code>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">datetime_format</td>
<td align="left">string / Integer</td>
<td align="left">Specifies the date format which will be used when converting to <code>DateTime</code> type. SQL Server format value is <code>20</code>. Snowflake format value <strong>when running from file uploads</strong> is <code>'YYYY-MM-DD hh24:mi:ss.ff3'</code>. When running Snowflake transformations direct from the source system, the format value must be <code>'YYYY-MM-DD hh24:mi:ss.ff3 TZHTZM'</code>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">starting_date</td>
<td align="left">string</td>
<td align="left">Specifies the starting date for currency conversions, when there are no prior historic exchange rates. This replaces the <code>null</code> value that is used in Salesforce.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Use_is_person_account</td>
<td align="left">Boolean</td>
<td align="left">Defines whether the IsPersonAccount attribute will be used. This should be disabled in Salesforce Orgs where there are no Person Accounts. Setting this to <code>true</code> will enable the attribute to being queried in the transformations, and will enable associated tests. Default is <code>false</code>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">use_currency_conversion</td>
<td align="left">Boolean</td>
<td align="left">Defines whether the multi currency conversion will be used. This should be disabled in Salesforce Orgs where multi currency is not used. Setting this to <code>true</code> will enable currency conversion. Default is <code>false</code>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">use_record_types</td>
<td align="left">Boolean</td>
<td align="left">Defines whether the record type conversions will be used. This should be disabled in Salesforce Orgs where record types are not used. Setting this to <code>true</code> will enable record types to be queried and added to the transformations. Default is <code>false</code>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">order_object_enabled</td>
<td align="left">Boolean</td>
<td align="left">Defines whether the order entity will be used. This should be disabled in Salesforce Orgs where orders are not used. Setting this to <code>true</code> will enable any transformations related to orders. Default is <code>false</code>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">quote_object_enabled</td>
<td align="left">Boolean</td>
<td align="left">Defines whether the quote entity will be used. This should be disabled in Salesforce Orgs where quotes are not used. Setting this to <code>true</code> will enable any transformations related to quotes. Default is <code>false</code>.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-adding-output-attributes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#adding-output-attributes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Adding output attributes</h3>
<p dir="auto">In order to add attributes, these should be related to the opportunity or any master data that is linked to the existing opportunity. These should be identified and linked using the OpportunityId field.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-adding-activities" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#adding-activities"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Adding activities</h3>
<p dir="auto">In order to add additional activities, it should be noted the CreateDate field is present in all tables and represents the moment in which a record was inserted in the table. This accurately represents the moment an entity was created, and in the object history tables, it represents the moment in which a record was modified.</p>
<p dir="auto">In case new fields need to be tracked, these need to be configured in Salesforce, and then added into the extraction filters in CData, and the Input tables. For example, if a new field such as <code>LeadSource</code> now needs to be tracked as an activity in the event log, then this should be added into the input <code>where</code> condition below:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="with Raw_leadhistory as (
    select * from {{ source(var(&quot;schema_sources&quot;), 'Raw_LeadHistory') }}
),

/* Input table for the lead history tracking file.
It contains lead history records. */
Leadhistory_input as (
    select
		-- Primary Key
		Raw_leadhistory.&quot;Id&quot; as &quot;Id&quot;,
		-- Table Fields
		Raw_leadhistory.&quot;CreatedById&quot; as &quot;Created_by_id&quot;,
		{{ pm_utils.to_timestamp('Raw_leadhistory.&quot;CreatedDate&quot;') }} as &quot;Created_date&quot;,
		Raw_leadhistory.&quot;Field&quot; as &quot;Field&quot;,
		Raw_leadhistory.&quot;LeadId&quot; as &quot;Lead_id&quot;,
		Raw_leadhistory.&quot;NewValue&quot; as &quot;New_value&quot;,
		Raw_leadhistory.&quot;OldValue&quot; as &quot;Old_value&quot;
    from Raw_leadhistory
	where Raw_leadhistory.&quot;Field&quot; in ('Status', 'Rating', 'Owner')

)

select * from Leadhistory_input"><pre>with Raw_leadhistory <span class="pl-k">as</span> (
    <span class="pl-k">select</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> {{ source(var(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>schema_sources<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>), <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Raw_LeadHistory<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) }}
),

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> Input table for the lead history tracking file.</span>
<span class="pl-c">It contains lead history records. <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
Leadhistory_input <span class="pl-k">as</span> (
    <span class="pl-k">select</span>
		<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Primary Key</span>
		Raw_leadhistory.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Table Fields</span>
		Raw_leadhistory.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>CreatedById<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Created_by_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		{{ <span class="pl-c1">pm_utils</span>.<span class="pl-c1">to_timestamp</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Raw_leadhistory."CreatedDate"<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) }} <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Created_date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		Raw_leadhistory.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Field<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Field<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		Raw_leadhistory.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>LeadId<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Lead_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		Raw_leadhistory.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>NewValue<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>New_value<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		Raw_leadhistory.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>OldValue<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Old_value<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    <span class="pl-k">from</span> Raw_leadhistory
	<span class="pl-k">where</span> Raw_leadhistory.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Field<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> (<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Status<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Rating<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Owner<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)

)

<span class="pl-k">select</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> Leadhistory_input</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The actual activity names will then need to be added into the events table for each existing entity, as shown below:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="with Leads as (
    select * from {{ ref('Lead') }}
),
Leads_history as (
    select * from {{ ref('LeadHistory_input') }}
),
Users as (
    select * from {{ ref('Users_input') }}
),

/* Define the change events for leads that are available in the entity table.
The activity name is based on the field that is changed and on the old and new value. */
Lead_change_events as (
    select
        -- Mandatory event attributes
        Leads.&quot;Lead_id&quot;,
        case
            when Leads_history.&quot;Field&quot; = 'Owner'
            then 'Change Lead Owner'
            when Leads_history.&quot;Field&quot; = 'Rating'
            then 'Change Lead Rating'
            else concat('Lead',' - ',Leads_history.&quot;New_value&quot;)
        end as &quot;Activity&quot;,
        Leads_history.&quot;Created_date&quot; as &quot;Event_end&quot;,
        -- Optional event attributes
        concat(Leads_history.&quot;Old_value&quot;,' to ',Leads_history.&quot;New_value&quot;) as &quot;Event_detail&quot;,
        Users.&quot;Name&quot;,
        Users.&quot;Department&quot; as &quot;Team&quot;,
        Users.&quot;User_type&quot; as &quot;User_type&quot;
    from Leads 
    inner join Leads_history
        on Leads.&quot;Lead_id&quot; = Leads_history.&quot;Lead_id&quot;
    left join Users
        on Leads_history.&quot;Created_by_id&quot; = Users.&quot;Id&quot;
)

select * from Lead_change_events
"><pre>with Leads <span class="pl-k">as</span> (
    <span class="pl-k">select</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> {{ ref(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Lead<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) }}
),
Leads_history <span class="pl-k">as</span> (
    <span class="pl-k">select</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> {{ ref(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>LeadHistory_input<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) }}
),
Users <span class="pl-k">as</span> (
    <span class="pl-k">select</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> {{ ref(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Users_input<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) }}
),

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> Define the change events for leads that are available in the entity table.</span>
<span class="pl-c">The activity name is based on the field that is changed and on the old and new value. <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
Lead_change_events <span class="pl-k">as</span> (
    <span class="pl-k">select</span>
        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Mandatory event attributes</span>
        Leads.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Lead_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
        case
            when Leads_history.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Field<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Owner<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
            then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Change Lead Owner<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
            when Leads_history.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Field<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Rating<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
            then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Change Lead Rating<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
            else concat(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Lead<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> - <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,Leads_history.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>New_value<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
        end <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Activity<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
        Leads_history.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Created_date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Event_end<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Optional event attributes</span>
        concat(Leads_history.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Old_value<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> to <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,Leads_history.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>New_value<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>) <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Event_detail<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
        Users.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Name<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
        Users.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Department<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Team<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
        Users.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>User_type<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>User_type<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    <span class="pl-k">from</span> Leads 
    <span class="pl-k">inner join</span> Leads_history
        <span class="pl-k">on</span> Leads.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Lead_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> Leads_history.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Lead_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    <span class="pl-k">left join</span> Users
        <span class="pl-k">on</span> Leads_history.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Created_by_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> Users.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
)

<span class="pl-k">select</span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> Lead_change_events
</pre></div>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-adding-entities" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#adding-entities"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Adding entities</h3>
<p dir="auto">Entities can be added by joining to any of the existing entities, and documenting the relationship in the <code>Entity_Relations</code> table.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-adding-business-data" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#adding-business-data"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Adding business data</h3>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Tags</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Tags can be added by creating an SQL which brings the <code>Opportunity_id</code> for any record that matches the tag criteria and adding into the <code>Tags_preprocessing</code> transformations. Each group of <code>Opportunity_id</code> is then added into a table with the corresponding tag name. Each query added should only bring the <code>Opportunity_id</code> and <code>Tag</code> fields.</p>
<p dir="auto">As an example, the following query retrieves records with multiple <code>Lead Owner</code> changes. This is a standalone query that only checks that specific condition. It identifies a specific activity, and groups by <code>Opportunity_id</code>, showing only records where that activity occurs more than one per <code>Opportunity_id</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Lead_owner_change_events as (
	select
		Opportunity_events.&quot;Opportunity_id&quot;
	from Opportunity_events
	where Opportunity_events.&quot;Activity&quot; = 'Change Lead Owner'
	group by Opportunity_events.&quot;Opportunity_id&quot;
	having count(*) &gt; 1
)"><pre>Lead_owner_change_events <span class="pl-k">as</span> (
	<span class="pl-k">select</span>
		Opportunity_events.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Opportunity_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
	<span class="pl-k">from</span> Opportunity_events
	<span class="pl-k">where</span> Opportunity_events.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Activity<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Change Lead Owner<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
	<span class="pl-k">group by</span> Opportunity_events.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Opportunity_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
	<span class="pl-k">having</span> <span class="pl-c1">count</span>(<span class="pl-k">*</span>) <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This will then be added via a <code>union all</code> statement together with all other tags which are identified in the transformations.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    -- Owner changed multiple times in leads
	select
		Lead_owner_change_events.&quot;Opportunity_id&quot;,
		'Lead owner changed multiple times' as &quot;Tag&quot;
	from Lead_owner_change_events
	union all
	-- Owner changed multiple times in orders
	select
		Order_owner_change_events.&quot;Opportunity_id&quot;,
		'Order owner changed multiple times' as &quot;Tag&quot;
	from Order_owner_change_events
	union all
	-- Opportunity Approval started multiple times
	select
		Opportunity_approval_started.&quot;Opportunity_id&quot;,
		'Approval process started multiple times' as &quot;Tag&quot;
	from Opportunity_approval_started"><pre>    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Owner changed multiple times in leads</span>
	<span class="pl-k">select</span>
		Lead_owner_change_events.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Opportunity_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Lead owner changed multiple times<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Tag<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
	<span class="pl-k">from</span> Lead_owner_change_events
	<span class="pl-k">union all</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Owner changed multiple times in orders</span>
	<span class="pl-k">select</span>
		Order_owner_change_events.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Opportunity_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Order owner changed multiple times<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Tag<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
	<span class="pl-k">from</span> Order_owner_change_events
	<span class="pl-k">union all</span>
	<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Opportunity Approval started multiple times</span>
	<span class="pl-k">select</span>
		Opportunity_approval_started.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Opportunity_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Approval process started multiple times<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Tag<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
	<span class="pl-k">from</span> Opportunity_approval_started</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The final output will look similar to this:</p>
<table>

<tr>
<th align="left">Case_ID</th>
<th align="left">Tag</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">0065f0000072kO5AAI</td>
<td align="left">Opportunity amount reduced</td>
</tr>

<td align="left">0065f0000072v2mAAA</td>
<td align="left">Opportunity amount reduced</td>
</tr>
