<p dir="auto"><strong>Due Dates</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Due dates can be added by identifying Actual and Expected dates for any event. Due to this being highly customizable by client, consideration should be taken to be able to group and consider multiple scenarios for one type of due date.</p>
<p dir="auto">To add a new due date, first prepare a query to bring the <code>Event_id</code>, the <code>Actual_date</code> in which the activity occurred, and the <code>Expected_date</code> in which the activity was supposed to occur.</p>
<p dir="auto">In the example below, the query is bringing records using the moment in which an opportunity is closed, as the actual date, and the Close Date as the expected date in which this was expected to happen.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="-- Define the expected close date as
    -- if there is no close date change then use the close date of the opportunity
    -- else use the first close date before change.
-- Define the actual close date as the last date in which the stage was changed (the moment in which the stage was changed to closed).
-- By filtering on Event_order_desc = 1 we are only picking up the last event, which will be the moment in which the opportunity is closed.
Original_close_date as (
    select
        Opportunity_event_log.&quot;Event_id&quot;,
        Opportunity.&quot;Last_stage_change_date&quot; as &quot;Actual_date&quot;,
        case
            when Opportunity_first_close_date.&quot;Min_close_date&quot; is null
            then {{ pm_utils.timestamp_from_date('Opportunity.&quot;Close_date&quot;')}}
            else Opportunity_first_close_date.&quot;Min_close_date&quot;
        end as &quot;Expected_date&quot;
    from Opportunity_event_log
    left join Opportunity
        on Opportunity_event_log.&quot;Opportunity_id&quot; = Opportunity.&quot;Opportunity_id&quot;
    left join Opportunity_first_close_date
        on Opportunity_first_close_date.&quot;Opportunity_id&quot; = Opportunity_event_log.&quot;Opportunity_id&quot;
    where Opportunity.&quot;Opportunity_closed&quot; = 1 and Opportunity_event_log.&quot;Event_order_desc&quot; = 1
)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Define the expected close date as</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> if there is no close date change then use the close date of the opportunity</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> else use the first close date before change.</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> Define the actual close date as the last date in which the stage was changed (the moment in which the stage was changed to closed).</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">--</span> By filtering on Event_order_desc = 1 we are only picking up the last event, which will be the moment in which the opportunity is closed.</span>
Original_close_date <span class="pl-k">as</span> (
    <span class="pl-k">select</span>
        Opportunity_event_log.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Event_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
        Opportunity.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Last_stage_change_date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Actual_date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
        case
            when Opportunity_first_close_date.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Min_close_date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> is <span class="pl-k">null</span>
            then {{ <span class="pl-c1">pm_utils</span>.<span class="pl-c1">timestamp_from_date</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Opportunity."Close_date"<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)}}
            else Opportunity_first_close_date.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Min_close_date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
        end <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Expected_date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    <span class="pl-k">from</span> Opportunity_event_log
    <span class="pl-k">left join</span> Opportunity
        <span class="pl-k">on</span> Opportunity_event_log.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Opportunity_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> Opportunity.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Opportunity_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    <span class="pl-k">left join</span> Opportunity_first_close_date
        <span class="pl-k">on</span> Opportunity_first_close_date.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Opportunity_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> Opportunity_event_log.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Opportunity_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    <span class="pl-k">where</span> Opportunity.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Opportunity_closed<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span> <span class="pl-k">and</span> Opportunity_event_log.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Event_order_desc<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note</strong>: In the example above, we identify the <code>Actual Date</code> using a specific logic, however, due dates can be defined using a specific activity name. In this case this was avoided as Salesforce allows significant customization and activity names might differ in different implementations.</p>
<p dir="auto">Once the due date logic is built, this then will be added into a table along with any other Due Date logics identified, also adding the name that will identify each logic. Additionally, any records which do not have any <code>Actual_date</code> or <code>Expected_date</code> values, will be excluded from the table.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-sql position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/* Table containing the due dates for the opportunity event log. */
Due_dates as (
	select 
		Original_close_date.&quot;Event_id&quot;,
		'Original Opportunity close date' as &quot;Due_date&quot;,
		Original_close_date.&quot;Actual_date&quot;,
		Original_close_date.&quot;Expected_date&quot;
	from Original_close_date
	where Original_close_date.&quot;Actual_date&quot; is not null and Original_close_date.&quot;Expected_date&quot; is not null
)"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span> Table containing the due dates for the opportunity event log. <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
Due_dates <span class="pl-k">as</span> (
	<span class="pl-k">select</span> 
		Original_close_date.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Event_id<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Original Opportunity close date<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Due_date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		Original_close_date.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Actual_date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
		Original_close_date.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Expected_date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
	<span class="pl-k">from</span> Original_close_date
	<span class="pl-k">where</span> Original_close_date.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Actual_date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">is not null</span> <span class="pl-k">and</span> Original_close_date.<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Expected_date<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">is not null</span>
)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The final output will look similar to this:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Event_id</th>
<th align="left">Due_date</th>
<th align="left">Actual_date</th>
<th align="left">Expected_date</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">26,520</td>
<td align="left">Original Opportunity close date</td>
<td align="left">2022-01-17 15:18:14.000</td>
<td align="left">2022-03-31 00:00:00.000</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">26,547</td>
<td align="left">Original Opportunity close date</td>
<td align="left">2022-01-17 15:18:14.000</td>
<td align="left">2022-03-31 00:00:00.000</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Other Configurations</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>Automated Users</code> and <code>Event Processing Estimates</code> seed files are provided as examples, and should be modified according to business requirements.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-limitations-known-issues-common-problems" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#limitations-known-issues-common-problems"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Limitations, known issues, common problems</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-limitations" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#limitations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Limitations</h3>
<p dir="auto"><strong>No history tracking on quote object</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">As of January 2022, this is a current limitation on the quote object in Salesforce, as it currently does not allow for field history tracking.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>No Event Start</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Salesforce does not store the start time for each change activity.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>No flag to identify automated users</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Salesforce does not have a field or special license for automated users. It does however have a default user named <code>Automated Process</code> which is used for automated processing for Salesforce changes, however any additional users such as interfaces or RPA will use normal licenses and are not differentiated by user type.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Salesforce Retention Policy</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">As of February 2022, Salesforce retains field history data for up to 18 months through the org and up to 24 months via the API.</p>
<p dir="auto">In case the history needs to be stored for a longer period of time, <a href="https://developer.salesforce.com/docs/atlas.en-us.securityImplGuide.meta/securityImplGuide/field_audit_trail.htm" rel="nofollow">Field Audit Trail</a> must be activated. This allows copying of history data into a separate big data object and allows storage for up to 10 years.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-known-issues" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#known-issues"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Known issues</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li></li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-common-problems" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#common-problems"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Common problems</h3>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-general" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#general"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>General</h4>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Field not available in object during data extraction</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Check Field Level Security in order to confirm the field is available and visible for the user profile extracting data. For <code>CurrencyISOCode</code>, <code>IsPersonAccount</code>, <code>LastStageChangeDate</code>, <code>RecordTypeId</code> check the specific issues in the following section.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Object not available during data extraction</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The user profile might not have read access to the object. This can be corrected on the user profile or a different user should extract the data. For <code>Order</code>, <code>Quote</code>, <code>CurrencyType</code>, <code>DatedConversionRate</code> check the specific issues in the following section.</p>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-object-specific" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#object-specific"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Object Specific</h4>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>Campaign</code> and <code>CampaignMember</code> objects not available</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Check the user record for the user extracting data, and verify the <code>Marketing User</code> checkbox is <code>Active</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>CurrencyISOCode</code> is not available when extracting data from the <code>Opportunity</code> object</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Multicurrency is not enabled within the Salesforce org. In case this happens, the conversions should be removed from the data model. This can be achieved by adjusting the variable <code>use_currency_conversion</code> in the <code>dbt_project.yml</code> to <code>false</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>CurrencyType</code> object is not available when extracting data</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Multicurrency is not enabled within the Salesforce org. In case this happens, the conversions should be removed from the data model. This can be achieved by adjusting the variable <code>use_currency_conversion</code> in the <code>dbt_project.yml</code> to <code>false</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>DatedConversionRate</code> object is not available when extracting data</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Effective currency rate management is not enabled within the Salesforce org. In case this happens, the conversions should be removed from the data model. This can be achieved by adjusting the variable <code>use_currency_conversion</code> in the <code>dbt_project.yml</code> to <code>false</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>IsPersonAccount</code> field not available in <code>Account</code> object when extracting from Salesforce</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">When extracting data from Salesforce, IsPersonAccount may not be available as the organization may not have B2C customers. In case this happens, the field should be removed from the data model. This can be achieved by adjusting the variable <code>use_is_person_account</code> in the <code>dbt_project.yml</code> to <code>false</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>LastStageChangeDate</code> field not available in <code>Opportunity</code> object when extracting from Salesforce</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The field <code>LastStageChangeDate</code> was only made available starting with Salesforce REST API <code>52.0</code>. Make sure the CData extraction or the extraction method used is using API <code>52.0</code> onwards.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>Order</code> object not available</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The Order object may not be enabled in the Salesforce org. In case this happens the table must be loaded empty to allow for all the rest of the transformations to occur. This can be achieved by adjusting the variable <code>order_object_enabled</code> in the <code>dbt_project.yml</code> to <code>false</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>Quote</code> object not available</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The Order object may not be enabled in the Salesforce org. In case this happens the table must be loaded empty to allow for all the rest of the transformations to occur. This can be achieved by adjusting the variable <code>quote_object_enabled</code> in the <code>dbt_project.yml</code> to <code>false</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>RecordTypeId</code> is not available when extracting data from the <code>Opportunity</code> object</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Record Types are not used within the Salesforce org. In case this happens, the conversions should be removed from the data model. This can be achieved by adjusting the variable <code>use_record_types</code> in the <code>dbt_project.yml</code> to <code>false</code>.</p>
</article>
  </div>

    </div>

  </readme-toc>
